rating:2.5
posted:Posted May 28, 2024
msg:Checkin 25 May 2024, we are a group of 3. We expect more comfort and breakfast from the previous review, however, the real experience we get:

Location: for us it is quite far from Yinheng station (Metro Line19) if you walk it take around 10-15min, more time if you have your luggage or walk to HZ east station quite far too. If you plan to travel around XiHu lake, we strongly NOT recommend this place, coz Didi takes around 30 min.  The only good thing is the supermarket, restaurant, tea shop, fast food are in the same place as the hotel.

Room: normal standard. Maybe because it has operated for a long time, but compared with the other new smaller  hotels in town or even the place we visit in wangxiangu, or huangling, those look more clean, comfort, air-flow than this hotel. Also the bathroom is normal. Walk way from elevator to the room can smell cigarettes.

Breakfast: Fail a lot. We went for breakfast around 8:45 am. There are Not much choices. Also we saw many food are run out of station, the staff not refill many of them. Staff who work at the noodle station look lot of tired, with sweat on her face, some of them not cover mask when speaking/cooking. 

Public toilet: it is located on the 13th floor (for hotel guest) Room for men is dirty and old. Only 1 room for guest on this floor in which for guests who come for breakfast, gym and laundry.

This hotel is a chain- hotel, room rental is not cheap, from our experience, we think the price we pay to other hotel can providd us the better location and foods


Total rating: 4/10

The overall feeling is quite good, it seems like a service that a 7-8 line city that needs lightning protection can provide!

The refreshing fragrance of flowers and plants in the rainy night speaks of the hospitality and warmth of "It is a great pleasure to have friends from afar". The herringbone canopy above the welcoming promenade gives passengers a zhengzheng oath to protect them from wind and rain.

Ms. Xiaohui, who was on duty at the front desk, gave me a warm reception and service with a smile. Not long after she handed her ID, she gave me the room card. Efficient and fast, give her a big compliment.

The hotel lobby is elegant and full of literary a**osphere. The sofa gets rid of the traditional middle-range style, boldly adopts modern elements, and the pillows are colorful, rendering the colorful journey time. The closets on both sides are full of books, so it is really suitable to sit on such a comfortable sofa and read some books for a while. A hotel with a book must be a hotel with feelings.

There are hollow screens on one side of the corridor leading to the passenger elevator, and abstract paintings hung on one side. There is a lamp under each screen, which adds to the new Chinese style of the hotel. These lights, just like the small orange lights described by Mr. Bing Xin, illuminate the passengers on the "home" road.

The rooms are also more exquisite and clean. The same is a wooden coffee table, chair, desk, rich Chinese elements. Open the curtains and you can see the view of the city. The night here is quiet, you can rest assured to wake up naturally.

The breakfast restaurant is elegant in style, and the various dining areas are neat and orderly, including the noodle area, the cooking area, the special snack area (smoked fish and lemon chicken feet are really unique), the pastry area, and the fruit salad area. The table lamp on the restaurant deck is half-hung, and it is a bit of an artistic conception of "coming out after a thousand calls, still holding the pipa half-hidden", waiting for food and waiting for the beautiful woman.

"I'm in Junting Hotel, I love Junchiguan quiet", when you come to Hangzhou East, Huihe Junting Hotel will be a home away from home.
